Unit identifier and unit type are not reported.\n\nOther dates and locations:\n\n     The date of the procedure is recorded as effectiveTime in the Procedure Details Clinical Statement in a Procedure Report  (V2).\n\nOther notes: The procedure id is recorded in the Procedure Details Clinical Statement in a Procedure Report (V2).
